        save_temporary_value_as = state_air_travel_consumption_prediction
        value = market_air_travel_production_if_no_pmg_base_building_airport
        add = scope:pm_international_routes_air_travel_prediction
        save_temporary_value_as = market_air_travel_production_prediction
        value = market_air_travel_consumption_if_no_pmg_base_building_airport
        save_temporary_value_as = market_air_travel_consumption_prediction
        value = air_travel_price_prediction
        multiply = scope:pm_international_routes_air_travel_prediction
    }
    divide = level
}

pmg_base_building_airport_pm_international_routes_profit_prediction_weighted = {
    value = pmg_base_building_airport_pm_international_routes_profit_prediction
